<text>I hurt my hip flexor/quad (pulled muscle or tear) and even after two weeks of intense pain, no movement (could barely take a step!), it wasn't getting better. I went to Ravive Health & Vitality for a cryotherapy session - doubts in mind, but since the rate was better than anywhere else, I figured "why not?"... it was AMAZING! First, it's incredibly relaxing and doesn't feel shocking or uncomfortable like ice packs. Second, it's so quick and easy-about 10 minutes laying on a massage table while the friendly practitioner directed the cool air on my injury to work its magic. This was on a Wednesday afternoon, and I didn't notice a big difference until Saturday morning when I went to yoga. Didn't wince once AND could even walk (at a slow pace) without any pain! It's been a week and a half and I've gotten consistently better. The past week, I resumed my daily yoga routine, could walk to do errands and could go up/down stairs! I 100% recommend Ravive Health & Vitality - not just for their cryotherapy, but also for their many other wellness services. <userid>104326562839335101890</userid><Name>Marilyn Monday</Name><Time>1609822938443< /Time><rating>5<//rating><text>You can do this hike in an hour (the long, gradual trail), OR you can go for the 282 uneven stone stairs and hit the top and back in 20 minutes. It's almost harder coming down, though, because by then your legs are tired and if it's cold out, mine cramp up so I feel like I might just buckle and tumble! There are several open landings where you can step aside and catch your breath.

Apparently the record for someone getting up the fastest was only 2 minutes, but Jesus f, that seems insane to me!!

There's a public restroom that's open at the top, but the visitors center is closed for now. Pretty crowded, there's really no avoiding people on the stairs, but most people were wearing masks when we went today - mine was damp by the end, though, because it's a real workout.
There seem to be a lot of kids who stand in the middle of pathways, and seem to be unaware that the stairs are difficult at all,  haha! If you're very worried about social distancing and masks, be aware that kids are being some real kids out there and will bump into you and not notice they're huffing and puffing right at you... You've gotta run your defense and just avoid getting close to 'em.

TOTALLY worth a stop!! We even found a meter that someone had paid ahead, still had 2.5 hours left on it when we left! A nice quick thing to conquer just to say ya did it.<//text>< Pics>

So sad in this day and age of Restaurants Galore that Waba Grill has become the latest price gouger out there. Is Gouger even a word? Perhaps Not.  Walked in here tonight with the intention of getting my Grub on... sadly it would Not happen. Waited a couple of minutes for the girl to come to the register. Noticed prices went up (not terribly, just a few cents here and there).  Went to order my staple, The Waba Signature Plate.  Was told, quite rudely, that I would have to pay Extra since I didn't want Rice. Sure, penalize me for wanting to be healthy. No More Waba for me!! I'm done with them. So sad cause I really liked their food. However, with an extra charge for being healthy  and a side of attitude, No Thank you.  Judging by the crowd in there.  2 people, they Probably could've used my order of 8 Plates!  Hungry family at home will Now be disappointed.  However with 10 Gazillion places to eat out there, I'm sure I'll find a substitute.

Waba Grill's Motto:

At WaBa Grill we are committed to providing our customers an enjoyable dining experience, serving the finest quality meals.

Our foundation is based on healthy eating with low calorie, low carb and high protein options.

We are the place for healthy food options on-the-go.

Lesson 1) Don't have an attitude with your customer.
Lesson 2) Don't boast "Eating Smart and Being Healthy"  then penalize a customer for wanting to do Just That.
Lesson 3) There are MANY places that offer Healthy Food Options on-the-go!

Connor</username><gmapID>0x80d954f6e2a7ed6f:0x5cf3d08bf850b37e<//gmapID><UserId.>112882266989280589474<//UserId.><response>None< /response><Rate>5</Rate><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPufQ41sPizPOYQrWe88iTZd65CXWaq6iarDH2c=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMNdF1dPZpwKzqeciq00dYfstsIMg4yDJX7EhiM=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM5IDTdlPiJ3OOxzrxVyKr0sB_1jw1jQUZUwwmL=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</Pics>< Review>
I'm a fairly regular patron of Redwing and have been for many years.  It is one of the best dive bars in San Diego that recently (about a year ago) got a bit of a refresh.  It did not lose it's neighbourhood charm with the refresh though, thankfully.  Tracy is my fave bartender!  She remembers everyone even when you haven't been in the bar in a year.  Somehow she even remembers how I love my turkey burger.  That brings me to my point: Redwing turkey burgers are the best burger in San Diego.  That is not an exaggeration either.  I don't eat red meat and I hate veggie burgers well because they're always terrible and the black bean burgers are usually tasteless but when I found the turkey burger at RBG I ate one every day for about 2 weeks.  I've turned hardcore carnivores into a lover of these burgers, too!  I'm sure it is the juices and stuff on the grill from everything else that makes these so delicious but who cares they are...they should be sampled by everyone.  They are always perfectly cooked with the right amount to char and are always super juicy and importantly they are not flattened to death by the chef.
RBG has great drink prices and happy hours plus there is a fantastic jukebox and they have karaoke a couple/few times a week.  If you come in and it's a bit crowded make your way straight through the bar out to the patio where there is a second bar.  The patio bar is usually open Friday through Sunday.< /Review>

This is an extremely lovable hole in the wall where some of the best nights of my life have taken place. The atmosphere is fun and welcoming no matter who you are or where your from. Whether your there to sing, dance or just watch, there karaoke nights are an absolute blast; even better, it happens 7 nights a week. It is a tiny space, and after a certain hour it gets super packed; usually with attractive people so the close proximity doesn't bother me. I will say, though that this becomes an issue for any woman that needs to use the restroom. There's only one stall and almost always a line. < review>
Redwing is supposed to be the 'gay bar' on North Park but in the last year (2013-2014) it's definitely become overrun with hipsters and straight allies.  Now don't me wrong I'm down with hipsters and allies but damn don't take over queer spaces y'all.

That aside they have a decent sized back patio (smoking section) and AC inside with several TV to watch the game.  They've also started carrying more craft beer and Thursday nights they have great trivia.

This is the place you want to karaoke!!!!  They have a good selection of songs and karaoke almost every night.</review>

<time>1522444493033<//time><Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
This is a great neighborhood bar with great food in a great neighborhood. Every bartender I've met so far has got a great personality and are happy to include you in conversations with other new folks and regulars.

I've been twice and had the wings both times and they were excellent also have a dish they called Chick A Rones which are chicken thigh and skin cook very crispy like a chicharron and with a spicy dipping sauce. This is a really excellent dish. I'm looking forward to going back and try new dishes.
I do want to mention that one of the sauces that they offer for dipping or salads or whatever is a cilantro cream sauce which as a lover of cilantro I can highly recommend.

They have lots of lots of different beers on tap as well as the old standby as in bottle and can, I especially like the selection of tall boys  they offer, especially if you like to drink old school!!</Text>
